SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_STARTING-BIT=0
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_CONSTANT-MASK=0xFFFF
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_METHOD=DIFF
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_SCALE=1 
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_REPORTER=CPU_PKGC_DBG_REPORTER
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_GROUP=00)Pkg C-state Entrance Count
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_OUTPUT-LABEL=Pkg C-state Entrance Count_C0 EntryCnt
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_COMMENT=Number of times PCU entered PKG C0
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_TIMELINE-FILE=pkgc_tl
# -->START EXCLUDE FROM NDA
SKL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_COMMENT=PKGC_C0_ENTRANCE_COUNTER
# <--END EXCLUDE FROM NDA

SKL_00)Pkg C-state Entrance Count_GROUP_SUMMARY-PRE-MSG=Note: Each C state EntryCnt counts only new entries to the state after collection started (does not count the initial state when collection started). Therefore it is possible to have 100% residency in C0 but see 0 Total occurrences for C0 because it remained in the same state.

KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_STARTING-BIT=0
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_CONSTANT-MASK=0xFFFF
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_METHOD=DIFF
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_SCALE=1 
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_REPORTER=CPU_PKGC_DBG_REPORTER
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_GROUP=00)Pkg C-state Entrance Count
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_OUTPUT-LABEL=Pkg C-state Entrance Count_C0 EntryCnt
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_COMMENT=Number of times PCU entered PKG C0
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_TIMELINE-FILE=pkgc_tl
# -->START EXCLUDE FROM NDA
KBL_ C0 EntryCnt_1_COMMENT=PKGC_C0_ENTRANCE_COUNTER
# <--END EXCLUDE FROM NDA

KBL_00)Pkg C-state Entrance Count_GROUP_SUMMARY-PRE-MSG=Note: Each C state EntryCnt counts only new entries to the state after collection started (does not count the initial state when collection started). Therefore it is possible to have 100% residency in C0 but see 0 Total occurrences for C0 because it remained in the same state.
